# <a name="required-diagnostic-data-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-103">Obavezni dijagnostički podaci za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-103">Required diagnostic data for Office</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-104">Informacije u ovom članku se odnose na verziju 1904 ili noviju, sledećih Office klijentskih softvera instaliranih na računaru sa operativnim sistemom Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-104">The information in this article applies to Version 1904 or later of the following Office client software installed on a computer running Windows:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-105">Office 365 ProPlus i Office 365 Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-105">Office 365 ProPlus and Office 365 Business</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home ili druge verzije sistema Office koje su deo pretplate na Office 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home, or other versions of Office that are part of an Office 365 subscription.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-107">Project i Visio koji se dobijaju uz neke planove pretplata, kao što je plan za Project Online Professional ili Visio Online Plan 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-107">Project and Visio that come with some subscription plans, such as the Project Online Professional plan or Visio Online Plan 2.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-108">Dijagnostički podaci se koriste da bi Office bio bezbedan i ažuriran, da bi se otkrili i otklonili problemi i da bi se poboljšao proizvod.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-108">Diagnostic data is used to keep Office secure and up-to-date, detect, diagnose and fix problems, and also make product improvements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-109">Ti podaci ne sadrže korisničko ime ili adresu elektronske pošte, sadržaj korisničkih datoteka ili informacije o aplikacijama nevezanim za Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-109">This data does not include a user’s name or email address, the content of the user’s files, or information about apps unrelated to Office.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-110">Ovi dijagnostički podaci se prikupljaju i šalju korporaciji Microsoft o Office klijentskom softveru koji se koristi na Windows računarima.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-110">This diagnostic data is collected and sent to Microsoft about Office client software being used on computers running Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-111">Neki dijagnostički podaci su obavezni, a neki su opcionalni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-111">Some diagnostic data is required, while some diagnostic data is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-112">Možete da izaberete da li ćete nam slati obavezne ili opcionalne dijagnostičke podatke pomoću kontrole privatnosti, kao što su postavke smernica organizacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-112">We give you the ability to choose whether to send us required or optional diagnostic data through the use of privacy controls, such as policy settings for organizations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-113">Možete da vidite dijagnostičke podatke koji nam se šalju koristeći prikaz dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-113">You can see the diagnostic data being sent to us by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-114">***Obavezni dijagnostički podaci*** su minimalni podaci neophodni da bi Office bio bezbedan, ažuriran i da radi kao što se očekuje na uređaju na kome je instaliran.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-114">***Required diagnostic data*** is the minimum data necessary to help keep Office secure, up-to-date, and performing as expected on the device it’s installed on.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-115">Obavezni dijagnostički podaci pomažu u identifikovanju problema sa sistemom Office koji su možda povezani sa konfiguracijom uređaja ili softvera.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-115">Required diagnostic data helps to identify problems with Office that may be related to a device or software configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-116">Na primer, oni mogu da pomognu da odredite da li neka funkcija sistema Office pada češće na određenoj verziji operativnog sistema, zbog novih funkcija, ili kada su određene funkcije sistema Office onemogućene.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-116">For example, it can help determine if an Office feature crashes more frequently on a particular operating system version, with newly introduced features, or when certain Office features are disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-117">Obavezni dijagnostički podaci pomažu nam da otkrijemo, ustanovimo i rešimo probleme brže, tako da se smanji uticaj na korisnike ili organizacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-117">Required diagnostic data helps us detect, diagnose, and fix these problems more quickly so the impact to users or organizations is reduced.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-118">Za više informacija o dijagnostičkim podacima pogledajte sledeće članke:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-118">For more information about diagnostic data, see the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-119">Opcionalni dijagnostički podaci za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-119">Optional diagnostic data for Office</span></span>](optional-diagnostic-data.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-120">Korišćenje Prikazivača dijagnostičkih podataka uz Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-120">Using the Diagnostic Data Viewer with Office</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/cf761ce9-d805-4c60-a339-4e07f3182855)

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-121">Ako ste administrator organizacije, možda će vas zanimati i sledeće:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-121">If you’re the admin for your organization, you might also be interested in the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-122">Pregled kontrola privatnosti za Office 365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-122">Overview of privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](overview-privacy-controls.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-123">Korišćenje regulatornih postavki za upravljanje kontrolama privatnosti u programu Office 365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-123">Use policy settings to manage privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](manage-privacy-controls.md)

## <a name="categories-data-subtypes-events-and-data-fields-for-required-diagnostic-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-124">Kategorije, podtipovi podataka, događaji i polja podataka za obavezne dijagnostičke podatke</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-124">Categories, data subtypes, events, and data fields for required diagnostic data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-125">Obavezni dijagnostički podaci organizovani su u kategorije i podtipove podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-125">Required diagnostic data is organized into categories and data subtypes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-126">U okviru svakog podtipa podataka su događaji koji sadrže polja podataka koja su specifična za taj događaj.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-126">Within each data subtype are events, which contain data fields that are specific to that event.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-127">Sledeća tabela sadrži listu kategorija za obavezne dijagnostičke podatke.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-127">The following table provides a list of the categories for required diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-128">Navedeni su podtipovi podataka u okviru svake kategorije, uz opis fokusa za taj podtip podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-128">The data subtypes within each category are listed, along with a description of the focus for that data subtype.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-129">Postoje veze do svakog odeljka podtipa podataka gde ćete pronaći sledeće informacije:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-129">There are links to each data subtype section where you’ll find the following information:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-130">Liste događaja u tom podtipu podataka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-130">A list of events in that data subtype</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-131">Opis svakog događaja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-131">A description of each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-132">Listu polja sa podacima u svakom događaju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-132">A list of data fields in each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-133">Opis svakog polja sa podacima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-133">A description of each data field</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="2505b-134">**Kategorija**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-134">**Category**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="2505b-135">**Podtip podataka**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-135">**Data subtype**</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="2505b-136">**Opis**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-136">**Description**</span></span>    |
| ---------- | ------------- | ---- |
| <span data-ttu-id="2505b-137">**Podešavanje softvera i popis**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-137">**Software setup and inventory**</span></span> | [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-138">Podešavanje sistema Office i popis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-138">Office setup and inventory</span></span>](#office-setup-and-inventory-subtype)   | <span data-ttu-id="2505b-139">Instalirani proizvod, verzija i status instalacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-139">Installed product and version and the installation status.</span></span>  |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-140">Konfiguracija Office programskih dodataka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-140">Office add-in configuration</span></span>](#office-add-in-configuration-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="2505b-141">Softverski dodaci i njihova podešavanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-141">Software add-ins and their settings.</span></span>     |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-142">Bezbednost</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-142">Security</span></span>](#security-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="2505b-143">Uslovi pod kojima dolazi do greški u dokumentima, funkcijama i dodacima a koje mogu da ugroze bezbednost, uključujući spremnost proizvoda za ažuriranje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-143">Document, feature, and add-in error conditions that may compromise security, including product update readiness.</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="2505b-144">**Upotreba proizvoda i usluga**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-144">**Product and service usage**</span></span>    | [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-145">Uspešnost funkcija aplikacije</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-145">Application feature success</span></span>](#application-feature-success-subtype)   | <span data-ttu-id="2505b-146">Uspešnost funkcionalnosti aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-146">Success of application functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-147">Ograničena na otvaranje i zatvaranje aplikacije i dokumenata, uređivanje i deljenje (saradnju) datoteka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-147">Limited to opening and closing of the application and documents, file editing, and file sharing (collaboration).</span></span> |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-148">Status aplikacije i pokretanje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-148">Application status and boot</span></span>](#application-status-and-boot-subtype)    | <span data-ttu-id="2505b-149">Utvrđivanje da li su se određene funkcije događaja odigrale, kao što su pokretanje ili zaustavljanje i da li funkcija radi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-149">Determination if specific feature events have occurred, such as start or stop, and if feature is running.</span></span>   |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-150">Konfiguracija pristupačnosti sistema Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-150">Office accessibility configuration</span></span>](#office-accessibility-configuration-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="2505b-151">Funkcije pristupačnosti u sistemu Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-151">Office accessibility features</span></span>       |
| <span data-ttu-id="2505b-152">**Performanse proizvoda i usluga**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-152">**Product and service performance**</span></span>       | [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-153">Neočekivani izlaz iz aplikacije (pad)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-153">Unexpected application exit (crash)</span></span>](#unexpected-application-exit-crash-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="2505b-154">Neočekivani izlazi (padovi) iz aplikacije i njeno stanje u trenutku kada se to dogodi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-154">Unexpected application exits and the state of the application when that happens.</span></span>    |
|  | [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-155">Performanse funkcija aplikacije</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-155">Application feature performance </span></span>](#application-feature-performance-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="2505b-156">Loše vreme odziva ili performansi u scenarijima kao što su pokretanje aplikacije ili otvaranje datoteke.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-156">Poor response time or performance for scenarios such as application start up or opening a file.</span></span> |
|  | [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-157">Greška u aktivnosti aplikacije</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-157">Application activity error</span></span>](#application-activity-error-subtype)   | <span data-ttu-id="2505b-158">Greške u funkcionalnosti funkcije ili korisničkog iskustva.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-158">Errors in functionality of a feature or user experience.</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="2505b-159">**Povezivanje uređaja i konfiguracija**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-159">**Device connectivity and configuration**</span></span> | [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-160">Povezivanje uređaja i konfiguracija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-160">Device connectivity and configuration</span></span>](#device-connectivity-and-configuration-subtype) | <span data-ttu-id="2505b-161">Stanje mrežne veze i podešavanje uređaja, kao što je memorija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-161">Network connection state and device settings, such as memory.</span></span> |


> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-162">Kategorije su prikazane u prikazivaču dijagnostičkih podataka, ali podtipovi podataka se ne prikazuju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-162">Categories are shown in the Diagnostic Data Viewer, but data subtypes are not shown.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-163">Polje podataka koje je označeno kao *Zastarelo* je ili će uskoro biti uklonjeno iz obaveznih dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-163">A data field marked *Obsolete* has been or will soon be removed from required diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-164">Neka od ovih polja podataka su duplikati koji su se pojavili u toku procesa modernizovanja dijagnostičkih podataka i koristili su se da osiguraju neometano funkcionisanje izveštaja aktivnog dijagnostičkog nadgledanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-164">Some of these data fields are duplicates that arose as diagnostic data was modernized and were used to ensure no service disruption to live diagnostic monitoring reports.</span></span>

## <a name="categories-and-data-fields-that-are-common-for-all-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-165">Kategorije i polja podataka koje su zajedničke za sve događaje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-165">Categories and data fields that are common for all events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-166">Postoje određene informacije o događajima koje su zajedničke za sve događaje, bez obzira na kategoriju ili podtip podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-166">There is some information about events that is common to all events, regardless of category or data subtype.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-167">Ove zajedničke informacije, koje se ponekad nazivaju *ugovori podataka*, organizovane su u kategorije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-167">This common information, which is sometimes referred to as *data contracts*, is organized into categories.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-168">Svaka kategorija sadrži polja, a ova polja čine metapodatke i svojstva pojedinačnih događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-168">Each category contains fields, and these fields are the metadata and properties of an individual event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-169">Možete da vidite ove informacije tako što ćete koristiti „Prikazivač dijagnostičkih podataka“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-169">You can view this information by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-170">Kategorije prikupljenih informacija o događajima mogu biti podeljene u dve grupe:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-170">The categories of information that is collected about events can be divided into two groups:</span></span>

  - [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-171">Informacije koje su zajedničke za sve događaje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-171">Information common to all events</span></span>](#information-common-to-all-events)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="2505b-172">Informacije koje posebno podržavaju prikupljanje dijagnostičkih podataka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-172">Information that specifically supports diagnostic data collection</span></span>](#information-that-specifically-supports-diagnostic-data-collection)

### <a name="information-common-to-all-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-173">*Informacije koje su zajedničke za sve događaje*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-173">*Information common to all events*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-174">Informacije koje su zajedničke za sve događaje se prikupljaju u sledećim kategorijama.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-174">Information common to all events is collected in the following categories.</span></span>

#### <a name="app"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-175">Aplikacija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-175">App</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-176">Informacije o aplikaciji.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-176">Information about the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-177">Sva polja su konstantna za sve sesije određene verzije aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-177">All fields are constant for all sessions of a given application version.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-178">Ova kategorija sadrži sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-178">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-179">**Grana** -Grana na kojoj je nastala određena verzija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-179">**Branch** - The branch that the given build came from.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-180">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo na kojem je tipu grane određena verzija nastala tako da možemo da ispravno usmerimo popravke.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-180">Allows us to determine what type of branch a given build came from so that we can correctly target fixes.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-181">**Tip instalacije** – brojač koji utvrđuje način na koji je korisnik instalirao aplikaciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-181">**InstallType** - An enumerator that identifies how the user installed the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-182">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo da li određeni mehanizmi instalacije prave probleme koji se ne vide u drugim mehanizmima za instalaciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-182">Allows us to determine if specific install mechanisms are creating issues that are not seen in other installation mechanisms.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-183">**Ime** - ime aplikacije koja pruža podatke.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-183">**Name** - The name of the application that is providing the data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-184">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo koja aplikacija ima problem, tako da znamo kako da ga popravimo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-184">Allows us to identify which application is showing an issue so we know how to address it.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-185">**Platforma** - široka klasifikacija platforme na kojoj je aplikacija pokrenuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-185">**Platform** - The broad classification of the platform on which the app is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-186">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo na kojim platformama se javlja problem tako da možemo ispravno da damo prioritet rešavanju tog problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-186">Allows us to identify on which platforms an issue may be occurring so that we can correctly prioritize the issue.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-187">**Verzija** - verzija aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-187">**Version** - The version of the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-188">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo koje verzije proizvoda ispoljavaju problem tako da možemo ispravno da damo prioritet rešavanju tog problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-188">Allows us to identify which versions of the product are showing an issue so that we can correctly prioritize it.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-240">**Ogranak** - određuje ogranak proizvoda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-240">**Fork** - Identifies the fork of the product.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-241">Omogućava mehanizam za grupisanje podataka u okviru skupa verzija radi utvrđivanja problema vezanih za određeno izdanje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-241">Allows a mechanism to aggregate data across a set of build numbers to identify issues related to a given release.</span></span>

#### <a name="session"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-242">Sesija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-242">Session</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-243">Informacije o procesu sesije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-243">Information about the process session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-244">Sva polja su konstantna za ovu sesiju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-244">All fields are constant for this session.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-245">Ova kategorija sadrži sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-245">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-246">**AB konfiguracije** - određuje skup letova koji se izvršavaju u određenoj sesiji.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-246">**ABConfigs** - Identifies the set of flights that are running in a given session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-247">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo koji pojedinačni letovi se izvršavaju u sesiji, tako da možemo utvrditi da li je let izvor problema koji utiče na korisnike.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-247">Allows us to identify which individual flights are running on a session so that we can determine if a flight is the source of an issue impacting users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-248">**EcsETag** – indikator iz sistema letova koji predstavlja letove poslate na računar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-248">**EcsETag** - An indicator from the flighting system that represents the flights sent to the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-249">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo koji letovi mogu da utiču na određenu sesiju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-249">Allows us to identify what flights might be impacting a given session.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-250">**Zastavice** – zastavice za praćenje maske bitova koje se mogu primeniti na celu sesiju, trenutno prevashodno usmerene na uzorkovanje i opcije dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-250">**Flags** - Bitmask tracking flags applicable to an entire session, currently primarily focused on sampling and diagnostic data options.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-251">Omogućava nam da kontrolišemo ponašanje određene sesije u odnosu na dijagnostičke podatke koje ona generiše.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-251">Allows us to control how a given session behaves in relation to the diagnostic data that the session generates.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-252">**Id** – jedinstveno identifikuje određenu sesiju podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-252">**Id** - Uniquely identifies a given session of data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-253">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo uticaj problema procenom broja sesija na koje problem utiče i da li postoje funkcije koje su zajedničke za ove sesije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-253">Allows us to identify the impact of issues by evaluating the number of sessions that are impacted and if there are common features of those sessions.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-254">**Id utiska** - određuje skup letova koji se izvršavaju u određenoj sesiji.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-254">**ImpressionId** - Identifies the set of flights that are running in a given session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-255">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo koji pojedinačni letovi se izvršavaju u sesiji, tako da možemo utvrditi da li je let izvor problema koji utiče na korisnike.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-255">Allows us to identify which individual flights are running on a session so that we can determine if a flight is the source of an issue impacting users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-256">**Merenje omogućeno** – zastavica koja ukazuje na to da li se podaci trenutne sesije uzorkuju ili ne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-256">**MeasuresEnabled** - Flag indicating if the current sessions data is sampled or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-257">Omogućava nam da odredimo kako statistički proceniti podatke koji su prikupljeni u određenoj sesiji.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-257">Allows us to determine how to statistically evaluate the data that is gathered from the given session.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-258">**Id klijenta za uzimanje uzorka** - id klijenta koji se koristi za utvrđivanje da li je deo procesa uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-258">**SamplingClientId** - The id of the client used to determine if it is part of sampling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-259">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo zašto je pojedinačna sesija uključena ili isključena iz uzoraka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-259">Allows us to determine why an individual session was included or excluded from sampling.</span></span>

#### <a name="user"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-260">Korisnik</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-260">User</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-261">Pruža informacije o zakupcu za jedinice za čuvanje zaliha komercijalnog softvera.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-261">Provides tenant information for commercial software SKUs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-262">Ova kategorija sadrži sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-262">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-263">**Heš primarnog identiteta** – identifikator pod pseudonimom koji predstavlja trenutnog korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-263">**PrimaryIdentityHash** – A pseudonymous identifier that represents the current user.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-264">**Mesto primarnog identiteta** – tip identiteta sadržanog u hešu primarnog identiteta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-264">**PrimaryIdentitySpace** – The type of identity contained in the PrimaryIdentityHash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-265">Jedan od MASCID, OrgIdCID ili UserObjectId.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-265">One of MASCID, OrgIdCID or UserObjectId.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-266">**Grupa zakupca** - tip zakupca kome pripada pretplata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-266">**TenantGroup** - The type of the tenant that the subscription belongs to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-267">Omogućava nam da klasifikujemo probleme i otkrijemo da li je problem rasprostranjen ili izolovan u skupu korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-267">Allows us to classify issues and identify whether a problem is widespread or isolated to a set of users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-268">**ID zakupca** - zakupac sa kojim je povezana pretplata korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-268">**TenantId** - The tenant that a user’s subscription is tied to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-269">Omogućava nam da klasifikujemo probleme i otkrijemo da li je problem rasprostranjen ili izolovan u skupu korisnika ili u određenom zakupcu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-269">Allows us to classify issues and identify whether a problem is widespread or isolated to a set of users or a specific tenant.</span></span>

### <a name="information-that-specifically-supports-diagnostic-data-collection"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-270">*Informacije koje posebno podržavaju prikupljanje dijagnostičkih podataka*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-270">*Information that specifically supports diagnostic data collection*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-271">Informacije koje posebno podržavaju prikupljanje dijagnostičkih podataka se prikupljaju u sledećim kategorijama.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-271">Information that specifically supports diagnostic data collection is collected in the following categories.</span></span>

#### <a name="activity"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-272">Aktivnost</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-272">Activity</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-273">Informacije koje služe za razumevanje uspešnosti samog procesa prikupljanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-273">Information to understand the success of the collection event itself.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-274">Ova kategorija sadrži sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-274">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-275">**Režim grupisanja** - govori sistemu kako da grupiše rezultate aktivnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-275">**AggMode** - Tells the system how to aggregate activity results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-276">Omogućava nam da smanjimo količinu informacija koje se otpremaju sa računara korisnika tako što grupišemo rezultate aktivnosti u jedan događaj koji se šalje povremeno.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-276">Allows us to reduce the amount of information uploaded from a user’s machine by aggregating activity results into a single event that gets sent periodically.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-277">**Broj** - koliko puta se aktivnost izvršila ako se broj izračunava iz grupisanog događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-277">**Count** - The number of times the activity happened if the count is from an aggregated event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-278">Omogućava nam da odredimo koliko često se aktivnost uspešno ili neuspešno izvršila u odnosu na režim grupisanja aktivnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-278">Allows us to determine how often an activity succeeded or failed based on the aggregation mode of the activity.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-279">**CV** - vrednost koja određuje odnos između aktivnosti i podaktivnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-279">**CV** - A value that identifies the relationship between activities and sub-activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-280">Omogućava nam da obnovimo odnos između ugnežđenih aktivnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-280">Allows us to rebuild the relationship between nested activities.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-281">**Trajanje** - koliko vremena je bilo potrebno za izvršavanje aktivnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-281">**Duration** - The length of time the activity took to execute.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-282">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo probleme sa performansama koje negativno utiču na iskustvo korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-282">Allows us to identify performance issues that are negatively impacting the users experience.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-283">**Rezultat**.**Kod** - Aplikacijom određena šifra koja služi za identifikaciju određenih rezultata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-283">**Result**.**Code** - An application defined code to identify a given results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-284">Omogućava nam da odredimo preciznije detalje određenog neuspeha, kao što je kôd greške koji se može koristiti za klasifikaciju i rešavanje problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-284">Allows us to determine more specific details of a given failure such as a failure code that can be used to classify and fix issues.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-285">**Rezultat.Oznaka** - oznaka celog broja koji određuje lokaciju u kodu gde je rezultat generisan.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-285">**Result.Tag** - An integer tag that identifies the location in code where the result was generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-286">Omogućava nam da jasno odredimo lokaciju u kôdu na kojoj je rezultat generisan što omogućava klasifikaciju grešaka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-286">Allows us to distinctly identify the location in code where a result was generated which enables classification of failures.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-287">**Rezultat**.**Tip** - tip kôda rezultata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-287">**Result**.**Type** - The type of the result code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-288">Određuje koji tip koda rezultata je poslat tako da vrednost može da se ispravno tumači.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-288">Identifies what type of result code was sent so that the value can be correctly interpreted.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-289">**Uspeh** – zastavica koja označava da li je aktivnost uspešno izvršena ili ne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-289">**Success** - A flag indicating if the activity succeeded or failed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-290">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo da li se radnje koje korisnik preduzima u proizvodu uspešno izvršavaju ili ne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-290">Allows us to determine if actions the user takes in the product are succeeding or failing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-291">To nam omogućava da prepoznamo probleme koji utiču na korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-291">This allows us to identify issues that are impacting the user.</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-292">Aplikacija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-292">Application</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-293">Informacije o instalaciji aplikacije iz koje se događaji prikupljaju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-293">Information about the installation of the application from which the events are being gathered.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-294">Ova kategorija sadrži sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-294">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-295">**Arhitektura** - arhitektura aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-295">**Architecture** - The architecture of the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-296">Omogućava nam da klasifikujemo greške koje mogu biti specifične za arhitekturu aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-296">Let’s us classify errors that might be specific to an architecture of the application.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-297">**Verzija „Klikni i pokreni“ paketa** - broj verzije „Klikni i pokreni“ paketa putem kojeg je aplikacija instalirana.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-297">**Click2RunPackageVersion** - The version number of the Click-To-Run package that installed the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-298">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo koja verzija instalacionog programa je korišćena za instalaciju sistema Office tako da moćemo da utvrdimo probleme vezane za instalaciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-298">Allows us to identify which version of the installer was used to install Office so we can identify setup related issues.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-299">**Distribucioni kanal** - kanal putem kojeg je aplikacija implementirana.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-299">**DistributionChannel** - The channel where the app was deployed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-300">Omogućava nam da podelimo dolazne podatke kako bismo utvrdili da li problemi utiču na korisnike.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-300">Allows us to partition incoming data so we can determine if issues are impacting audiences.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-301">**Metod instalacije** - Da li je trenutna verzija sistema Office instalirana nadogradnjom, vraćanjem na prethodnu verziju ili novom instalacijom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-301">**InstallMethod** - Whether the current build of Office was upgraded from an older build, rolled back to an older build, or a fresh install.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-302">**Je „Klikni i pokreni“ instalacija** – zastavica koja ukazuje na to da li je instalacija tipa „Klikni i pokreni“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-302">**IsClickToRunInstall** - Flag indicating if install was a click to run install.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-303">Omogućava nam da prepoznamo probleme koje mogu biti specifični za mehanizam „Klikni i Pokreni“ instalacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-303">Allows us to identify issues that might be specific to the Click-To-Run install mechanism.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-304">**IsDebug** – zastavica koja ukazuje na to da li verzija sistema Office predstavlja izdanje za otklanjanje grešaka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-304">**IsDebug** - Flag indicating if the office build is a Debug build.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-305">Omogućava nam da otkrijemo da li problemi dolaze iz verzija za otklanjanje grešaka koje mogu da se ponašaju drugačije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-305">Allows us to identify if issues are coming from Debug builds which may behave differently .</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-306">**Je instalirano na spoljašnjem uređaju za skladištenje** – zastavica koja ukazuje na to da li je sistem Office instaliran na spoljašnjem uređaju za skladištenje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-306">**IsInstalledOnExternalStorage** - Flag indicating if Office was installed on an external storage device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-307">Omogućava nam da odredimo da li uzrok problema može biti vezan za spoljni prostor za skladištenje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-307">Let’s us determine if issues can be traced to an external storage location.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-308">**Je OEM Instalacija** – zastavica koja ukazuje na to da li je Office instalirao proizvođač originalne opreme (OEM).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-308">**IsOEMInstalled** - Flag indicating if Office was installed by an original equipment manufacturer (OEM).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-309">Omogućava nam da odredimo da li aplikaciju instalirao OEM, što nam pomaže da klasifikujemo i prepoznamo probleme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-309">Let’s us determine if the application was installed by an OEM which can help us classify and identify issues.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-310">**Prethodna verzija** - verzija sistema Office koja je prethodno bila instalirana na računaru.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-310">**PreviousVersion** - The version of Office that was previously installed on the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-311">Omogućava nam da vratimo prethodnu verziju ako aktuelna verzija ima problem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-311">Allows us to roll back to a previous version if the current one has an issue.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-312">**Ime izvršne datoteke procesa** - ime izvršne datoteke aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-312">**ProcessFileName** - The name of the application filename.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-313">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo ime izvršne datoteke koja generiše podatke pošto može postojati nekoliko različitih imena izvršne datoteke procesa koja se pojavljuju pod istim imenom aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-313">Allows us to identify the name of the executable which is generating the data as there may be several different process filenames reporting as the same app name.</span></span>

#### <a name="client"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-314">Klijent</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-314">Client</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-315">Informacije o Office aplikaciji.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-315">Information about the Office client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-316">Ova kategorija sadrži sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-316">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-317">**Vreme prvog pokretanja** – Kada je klijent prvi put pokrenut.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-317">**FirstRunTime** - The first time the client was run.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-318">Omogućava nam da razumemo koliko dugo je korisnik imao instaliran sistem Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-318">Allows us to understand how long the client has had Office installed.</span></span>

#### <a name="device"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-319">Uređaj</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-319">Device</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-326">**Veličina i oblik uređaja** - određuje koje veličine i oblika je uređaj koji šalje informacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-326">**FormFactorFamily** - Identifies what form factor the device sending the info is.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-327">Omogućava nam da klasifikujemo podatke na osnovu okretanja uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-327">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-328">**Horizontalna rezolucija** - horizontalna rezolucija ekrana uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-328">**HorizontalResolution** - The horizontal resolution of the devices screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-329">Omogućava nam da klasifikujemo podatke na osnovu okretanja uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-329">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-330">**Id** - jedinstveni identifikator uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-330">**Id** - A unique identifier for the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-331">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo distribuciju problema u skupu uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-331">Allows us to identify the distribution of issues across a set of devices.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-332">**Poboljšana zaštita podataka je omogućena** - zastavica koja označava da li je na računaru omogućena poboljšana zaštita podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-332">**IsEDPPolicyEnabled** - Flag to indicate if enhanced data protection is enabled on the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-333">Omogućava nam da klasifikujemo podatke na osnovu okretanja uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-333">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-336">**Proizvođač** - Proizvođač uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-336">**Manufacturer** - The manufacturer of the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-337">Omogućava nam da klasifikujemo podatke na osnovu okretanja uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-337">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-338">**Model** - model uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-338">**Model** - The model of the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-339">Omogućava nam da klasifikujemo podatke na osnovu okretanja uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-339">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-340">**UUIDHash matične ploče** - heš jedinstvenog identifikatora matične ploče.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-340">**MotherboardUUIDHash** - A hash of a unique identifier for the motherboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-341">Omogućava nam da klasifikujemo podatke na osnovu okretanja uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-341">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-344">**Broj fizičkih jezgara procesora** Broj fizičkih jezgara procesora računara.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-344">**NumProcPhysCores** - The number of physical cores on the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-345">Omogućava nam da klasifikujemo podatke na osnovu okretanja uređaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-345">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

#### <a name="event"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-370">Događaj</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-370">Event</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-371">Informacije specifične za određeni događaj, uključujući i njegov jedinstveni identifikator u okviru sesije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-371">Event-specific information, including its unique identifier in the session.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-372">Ova kategorija sadrži sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-372">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-373">**Ugovor** - Lista svih ugovora koji događaj sprovodi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-373">**Contract** - A list of any contracts that the event is implementing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-374">Omogućava nam da razmotrimo koji podaci su deo pojedinačnog događaja, tako da efikasno možemo da ih obradimo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-374">Allows us to evaluate what data is part of the individual event so that we can process it effectively.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-375">**CV** - Vrednost koja nam omogućava da identifikujemo događaje koji su povezani jedan sa drugim.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-375">**CV** - A value that allows us to identify events that are related to one another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-376">Koristi se za dijagnostiku da nam omogući da identifikujemo obrasce srodnog ponašanja ili srodnih događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-376">Used for diagnostics to allow us to identify patterns of related behavior or related events.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-377">**Zastavice** - Informacije koje se koriste da izmene način odgovara određenog događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-377">**Flags** - Information used to alter how a given event responds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-378">Koristi se za upravljanje načina na koji se određeni događaj tretira u svrhu otpremanja podataka korporaciji Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-378">Used to manage how a given event is treated for the purposes of uploading the data to Microsoft.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-379">**Id** - Jedinstveni identifikator događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-379">**Id** - A unique identifier for the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-380">Omogućava nam da jedinstveno identifikujemo događaje koji primamo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-380">Allows us to uniquely identify the events that are being received.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-381">**Ime** - Ime događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-381">**Name** - The name of the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-382">Omogućava da identifikujemo događaj koji je klijent poslao.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-382">Allows to identify the event that was being sent from the client.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-383">**Pravilo** – Identifikator pravila koji je generisao podatke ako su generisani po pravilu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-383">**Rule** - An identifier of the rule that generated the data if it was generated by a rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-384">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo izvor dela podataka, kako bismo mogli da proverimo valjanost i upravljamo parametrima tog događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-384">Allows us to identify the source of a piece of data so that we can validate and manage that events parameters</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-385">**Id pravila** – Identifikator pravila koje je generisalo podatke ako su generisani po pravilu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-385">**RuleId** - The identifier of the rule that generated the data if it was generated by a rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-386">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo izvor dela podataka, kako bismo mogli da proverimo valjanost i upravljamo parametrima tog događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-386">Allows us to identify the source of a piece of data so that we can validate and manage that events parameters.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-387">**Interfejs pravila** - Bilo koji interfejs koji određeno pravilo implementira.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-387">**RuleInterfaces** - Any interfaces that are implemented by the specific rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-388">Omogućava nam da klasifikujemo i uvezemo podatke zasnovane na njihovoj strukturu, što pojednostavljuje obradu podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-388">Allows us to classify and import the data based on its structure which simplifies data processing.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-389">**Verzija pravila** – Identifikator pravila koje je generisalo podatke ako su generisani po pravilu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-389">**RuleVersion** - The identifier of the rule that generated the data if it was generated by a rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-390">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo izvor dela podataka, kako bismo mogli da proverimo valjanost i upravljamo parametrima tog događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-390">Allows us to identify the source of a piece of data so that we can validate and manage that events parameters.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-391">**Učestalost uzorkovanja** – pokazatelj procenta korisnika koji šalju ovaj deo podataka. To nam omogućava da uradimo statističku analizu podataka i za vrlo česte tačke podataka ne zahteva slanje od svih korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-391">**SampleRate** - An indication of what percentage of users are sending this piece of data This allows us to do statistical analysis of the data and for very common data points not require that to be sent by all users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-392">**Verzija šeme** – Verzija šeme koja se koristi za generisanje dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-392">**SchemaVersion** - The version of the schema used to generate diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-393">Obavezno za upravljanje podacima koji šalje klijent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-393">Required to manage data being sent form the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-394">Ovo omogućava povremene promene podataka koje svaki klijent šalje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-394">This allows changes over time in what data is being sent from each client.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-395">**Redosled** - Brojač koji identifikuje redosled prema kojem je događaj generisan na klijentu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-395">**Sequence** - A counter that identifies the order that an event was generated on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-396">Omogućava da se primljeni podaci poređaju tako da možemo da utvrdimo koji su koraci možda doveli do problema koji utiče na klijente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-396">Allows the data being received to be ordered so that we can identify what steps may have led to an issue that is impacting clients.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-397">**Izvor** -Izvorni kanal koji je korišćen za otpremanje podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-397">**Source** - The source pipeline that was used to upload the data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-398">Obavezno za praćenje svih naš otpremnih kanala za celokupno zdravlje i za pomoć u prepoznavanju problema sa otpremnih kanala.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-398">Required to monitor each of our upload pipelines for overall health and to help identify issues with the upload pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-399">To nam omogućava praćenje pojedinačnih otpremnih kanala kako bismo obezbedili njihovu usaglašenost.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-399">This allows us to monitor individual upload pipelines to make sure they remain compliant.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-400">**Vreme** – Vreme generisanja događaja na klijentu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-400">**Time** - The time that the event was generated on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-401">Omogućava nam da sinhronizujemo i proverimo redosled događaja generisanih na klijentu, kao i da uspostavimo pokazatelje performansi za uputstva korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-401">Allows us to synchronize and validate the order of events generated on the client as well as establish performance metrics for user instructions.</span></span>

#### <a name="session"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-419">Sesija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-419">Session</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-420">Informacije o procesu sesije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-420">Information about the process session.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-421">Ova kategorija sadrži sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-421">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-422">**Delta AB konfiguracija** - Prati razlike između podataka trenutne AB konfiguracije i prethodne vrednosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-422">**ABConfigsDelta** - Tracks the difference between the current ABConfigs data and the previous value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-423">Omogućava nam da pratimo nove letove na računaru kako bi utvrdili da li je novi let odgovoran za problem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-423">Allows us to track what new flights are on the machine to help identify if a new flight is responsible for an issue.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-424">**Klasifikacija prikupljenih podataka** - Klase informacija koje sesija može da prikupi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-424">**CollectibleClassification** - The classes of information the session can collect.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-425">Omogućava filtriranje sesija na osnovu podataka koje bi one imale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-425">Allows filtering of sessions based on the data they would have.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-426">**Onemogućavanje telemetrije** – Zastavica koja ukazuje na to da li je aktiviran ključ za onemogućavanje telemetrije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-426">**DisableTelemetry** - Flag indicating if the DisableTelemetry key is set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-427">Omogućava nam da znamo ako sesija nije prijavljivala dijagnostičke podatke koji ne spadaju u metapodatke osnovnih usluga.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-427">Allows us to know if a session was not reporting diagnostic data other than EssentialServiceMetadata.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-428">**Ključ uzorkovanja** -ključ koji se koristi za određivanje da li je sesija uzorkovana ili ne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-428">**SamplingKey** - The key used to determine whether the session is sampled or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-429">Omogućava nam da razumemo kako pojedinačne sesije prave izbor da li su uzorkovane ili ne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-429">Allows us to understand how individual sessions are making their choice of whether they are sampled or not.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-430">**Metoda uzorkovanja** - Metoda koja se koristi za određivanje smernica za uzorkovanje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-430">**SamplingMethod** - The method used to determine sampling policy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-431">Omogućava nam da razumemo koji podaci potiču iz sesije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-431">Allows us to understand what data is coming from a session.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-432">**Redosled** - Jedinstveni numerički identifikator za sesiju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-432">**Sequence** - A unique numeric identifier for the session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-433">Omogućava uređivanje rasporeda sesija za analiziranje kada je možda došlo je do problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-433">Allows the ordering of sessions for analysis of then issues might have occurred.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-434">**Početak** – Vreme pokretanja procesa sesije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-434">**Start** - The boot time of the process session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-435">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo kada je sesija počela.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-435">Allows us to establish when the session started.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-436">**Razlika između vremenskih zona u minutima** - Razlika u minutima između lokalnog vremena i UTC vremena.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-436">**TimeZoneBiasInMinutes** - The difference in minutes between UTC and the local time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-437">Omogućava normalizaciju UTC vremena u lokalno vreme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-437">Allows normalization of UTC times back to the local time.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-438">**Id vrednost klijenta za uzorkovanje** - Vrednost ključa koji se koristi za određivanje uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-438">**SamplingClientIdValue** - The value of the key used to determine sampling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-439">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo zašto je sesija uzorkovana ili nije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-439">Allows us to determine why a session was sampled or not.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-440">**Id vrednost uređaja za uzorkovanje** - Vrednost ključa koji se koristi za određivanje uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-440">**SamplingDeviceIdValue** - The value of the key used to determine sampling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-441">Omogućava nam da utvrdimo zašto je sesija uzorkovana ili nije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-441">Allows us to determine why a session was sampled or not.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-442">**K vrednost uzorkovanja sesije** – Napredni metapodaci uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-442">**SamplingSessionKValue** - Advanced sampling metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-443">Koriste se za procenu statističkog značenja primljenih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-443">Used to help evaluate statistical meaning of data that is received.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-444">**N vrednost uzorkovanja sesije** – Napredni metapodaci uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-444">**SamplingSessionNValue** - Advanced sampling metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-445">Koriste se za procenu statističkog značenja primljenih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-445">Used to help evaluate statistical meaning of data that is received.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-446">**Nivo dozvole za telemetriju** – Vrednost koja ukazuje na nivo prikupljanja dijagnostičkih podataka koji je korisnik dozvolio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-446">**TelemetryPermissionLevel** - Value indicating what level of diagnostic data the user has opted into.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-447">Omogućava nam da razumemo koji nivo dijagnostičkih podataka da očekujemo od sesije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-447">Allows us to understand what level of diagnostic data to expect from a session.</span></span>

#### <a name="officecorrelationmetadatautccorrelationmetadata"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-465">Office.CorrelationMetadata.UTCCorrelationMetadata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-465">Office.CorrelationMetadata.UTCCorrelationMetadata</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-466">Prikuplja metapodatke sistema Office kroz UTC za poređenje sa ekvivalentnim podacima prikupljenim putem kanal Office telemetrije u cilju provere ispravnosti i potpunosti podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-466">Collects Office metadata through UTC to compare with equivalent data collected through the Office telemetry pipeline to check correctness and completeness of data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-467">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-467">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-468">**ab konfiguracije** - Lista ID-ova funkcija za utvrđivanje koje funkcije su omogućene na klijentu ili su prazne kada se ti podaci se ne prikupljaju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-468">**abConfigs** - A list of feature IDs to identify which features are enabled on the client or empty when this data is not being collected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-469">**abFlights** -„NoNL:NoFlights” kada letovi funkcija nisu podešeni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-469">**abFlights** - "NoNL:NoFlights" when the feature flights aren't set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-470">U suprotnom „holdoutinfo = nepoznato”.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-470">Otherwise "holdoutinfo=unknown".</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-471">**Guid sesije aplikacije** – identifikator sesije za određenu aplikaciju počevši od vremena kreiranja procesa do kraja procesa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-471">**AppSessionGuid** - An identifier of a particular application session starting at process creation time and persisting until process end.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-472">Oblikovan je kao standardni 128-bitni GUID, ali se sastoji iz 4 dela.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-472">It is formatted as a standard 128-bit GUID but constructed of 4 parts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-473">Ta četiri dela su po redu (1) 32-bitni ID procesa (2) 16-bitni ID sesije (3) 16-bitni ID za pokretanje (4) 64-bitni proces nastanka u UTC 100ns</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-473">Those four parts in order are (1) 32 bit Process ID (2) 16 bit Session ID (3) 16 bit Boot ID (4) 64 bit Process creation time in UTC 100ns</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-474">\*\*verzija izdanja aplikacije \*\* – Broj verzije izdanja aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-474">**appVersionBuild** - The app build version number.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-475">**appVersionMajor** - Broj glavne verzije aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-475">**appVersionMajor** - The app major version number.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-476">**sporedna verzija aplikacije** - Broj sporedne verzije aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-476">**appVersionMinor** - The app minor version number.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-477">**revizija verzije aplikacije** - Broj revizije verzije aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-477">**appVersionRevision** - The app revision version number.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-478">**Grupa korisnika** - Ime za grupu korisnika izdanja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-478">**audienceGroup** - The release audience group name</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-479">**Id korisnika** - Ime za korisnike izdanja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-479">**audienceId** - The release audience name</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-480">**kanal** - Kanal preko kog je distribuiran sistem Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-480">**channel** - The channel by which Office was distributed</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-482">**ecsETag** - Identifikator eksperimenta za proces</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-482">**ecsETag** - An experiment identifier for the process</span></span>

#### <a name="officetargetedmessagingensurecached"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-492">Office.TargetedMessaging.EnsureCached</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-492">Office.TargetedMessaging.EnsureCached</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-493">Prati da li je preuzet paket za „Dinamičko platno“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-493">Tracks if a package for Dynamic Canvas was downloaded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-494">Smatra se konfiguracijom softvera zato što paket mora biti uspešno preuzet da bi klijentu omogućio pružanje odgovarajućeg iskustva.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-494">Considered a software configuration because the package must be successfully downloaded to enable the client to render the right experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-495">Posebno je važno u korisničkim pretplatama gde platno koristimo da korisnika obavestimo da je licenca istekla.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-495">Is especially critical in consumer subscriptions where we use canvas to communicate to the user that the license has expired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-496">Koristi se za praćenje metapodataka paketa dinamičkog sadržaja koje proizvod preuzima i kešira, kao i rezultate operacija koje se izvršavaju na paketu: neuspela preuzimanja, neuspela raspakivanja, greške pri proveri doslednosti, pregledi keša, primene paketa, izvori preuzimanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-496">Used to track metadata of a dynamic content package downloaded and cached by the product as well as results of operations performed on the package: download failures, unpacking failures, consistency checks failures, cache hits, package usages, download sources.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-497">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-497">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-498">**Podaci\_Keš fascikla nije kreirana -** Bulova zastavica koja ukazuje na to da je kreiranje fascikle keša uspešno izvršeno</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-498">**Data\_CacheFolderNotCreated -** Boolean flag indicating if cache folder creation succeed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-499">**Podaci\_CdnPath – izvorna adresa paketa-**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-499">**Data\_CdnPath – source address of the package-**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-500">**Podaci\_EnsureCached -** Bulova zastavica koja ukazuje na to da li je paket sa sadržajem keširan</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-500">**Data\_EnsureCached -** Boolean flag indicating if content package was cached</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-501">**Podaci\_Već postoji -** Bulova zastavica koja ukazuje na to da je paket ranije već bio preuzet i da je napravljen još jedan pokušaj</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-501">**Data\_ExistsAlready -** Boolean flag indicating that the package was already downloaded before and there was another attempt</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-502">**Podaci\_Preuzimanje toka datoteka nije uspelo -** izvorni paket nije dostupan u izvoru</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-502">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailed -** source package not available in source</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-503">**Podaci\_Preuzimanje toka datoteka nije uspelo na kreira lokalnu fasciklu -** problemi na lokalnom disku izazivaju grešku prilikom kreiranja direktorijuma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-503">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailedToCreateLocalFolder -** local disk issues causing failure in directory creation</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-504">**Podaci\_Preuzimanje toka datoteka iz paketa nije uspelo -** zastavica koja označava da li je paket preuzet, ali ga klijent ne može pročitati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-504">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageFailed -** flag indicating if package was downloaded, but the client can’t read it</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-505">**Podaci\_Preuzimanje toka datoteka iz paketa je uspelo -** uspešni pokušaj čitanja paketa</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-505">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageSuccess -** successful attempts to read the package</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-506">**Podaci\_Preuzimanje toka datoteka je uspelo -** bez problema na disku ili problema sa konfiguracijom koja ne dozvoljava čitanje toka datoteka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-506">**Data\_GetFileStreamSuccess -** no disk issues nor configuration issues which doesn’t let the file stream to be read</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-507">**Podaci\_Preuzimanje relativne putanje nije uspelo -** relativna putanja ne upućuje na pristupačnu lokaciju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-507">**Data\_GetRelativePathsFailed -** relative path doesn’t point to accessible location</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-508">**Podaci\_Stvarna vrednost heša -** heš vrednost izdvojena iz imena datoteke kada je paket upotrebljen</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-508">**Data\_HashActualValue -** hash value extracted from file name when the package was used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-509">**Podaci\_Neuspešno izračunavanje heša -** greška pri izračunavanju heša</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-509">**Data\_HashCalculationFailed -** error with calculation of a hash</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-510">**Podaci\_HashMatchFailed -** nepodudaranje heša za ime paketa i keširanih vrednosti registratora</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-510">**Data\_HashMatchFailed -** hash mismatch between the package name and registry values cached</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-511">**Podaci\_HashMatchSuccess -** uspešna provera doslednosti heša</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-511">**Data\_HashMatchSuccess -** hash consistency check success</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-512">**Podaci\_Neuspeli zahtev za preuzimanje paketa -** preuzimanje paketa nije moguće</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-512">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestFailed -** can’t download the package</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-513">**Podaci\_Zahtev za preuzimanje paketa ne sadrži podatke -** preuzeti paket ne sadrži podatke</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-513">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestNoData -** downloaded package contains no data</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-514">**Podaci\_Uspešan zahtev za preuzimanje paketa -** uspešno preuzimanje paketa</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-514">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestSuccess -** successful download of a package</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-515">**Podaci\_Uspešno raspakivanje paketa -** statusi pokušaja raspakivanja </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-515">**Data\_PackageExplodedSuccess -** unpacking attempts statuses</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-516">**Podaci\_Otvaranje paketa nije uspelo -** neuspeli pokušaji otvaranja datoteke paketa</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-516">**Data\_PackageOpenFailed -** failed attempts to open the package file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-517">**Podaci\_Uspešno otvaranje paketa -** uspešni pokušaji otvaranja datoteke paketa</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-517">**Data\_PackageOpenSuccess -** successful attempts to open the package file</span></span>
