#### <a name="officefileiocsiccachedfilecsisavefilebasic"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-933">Office.FileIO.CSI.CCachedFileCsiSaveFileBasic</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-933">Office.FileIO.CSI.CCachedFileCsiSaveFileBasic</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-934">Omogućava nam da znamo da li je datoteka uspešno sačuvana iz FIO sloja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-934">Allows us to know if a file was successfully saved from the FIO Layer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-935">Koristi se za nadgledanje i ispravnost funkcija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-935">Used for Feature Health and monitoring.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-936">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-936">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-937">**Grupa aktivnosti -** oznaka koja omogućava da skup događaja za praćenje bude grupisan kako bi upravljao sveukupnim uspehom</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-937">**Activity.Group -** tag that allows a set of monitoring events to be grouped to manage overall success</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-938">**Activity.IsHVA -** zastavica koja označava da je događaj ključan za uspeh korisnika</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-938">**Activity.IsHVA -** flag to indicate that event is critical to user success</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-939">**Data.AsyncOpen -** zastavica koja označava da je otvoren dokument sa sadržajem koji je stigao posle otvaranja glavnog tela</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-939">**Data.AsyncOpen -** flag to indicate that the document was opened with content that arrived after the main body was opened</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-940">**Data.BaseDownloadTriggered -** Promena praćenja dijagnostike koja ukazuje na to da je zatražena osnovna verzija dokumenta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-940">**Data.BaseDownloadTriggered -** Change tracking diagnostic indicating that the base version of the document was requested</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-941">**Data.BlockAutoUploadReasons -** kodove razloga za blokiran status otpremanja (npr. Automatsko čuvanje je isključeno, dokument je u tranziciji)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-941">**Data.BlockAutoUploadReasons -** Reason codes for blocked upload state (e.g. Autosave is turned off, the document is transitioning)</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-942">**Data.BlockUploadDueToFailedSaveAsOverExisting -** Otpremanje je blokirao jer će biti neuspešno pri ponovnom pokušaju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-942">**Data.BlockUploadDueToFailedSaveAsOverExisting -** Upload is blocked as it would fail if retried</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-943">**Data.CacheFileId -** se povezuje sa telemetrijom keša Office dokumenata da omogući analizu uticaja problema sa kešom na korisničko iskustvo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-943">**Data.CacheFileId -** connects to Office Document Cache telemetry to enable impact analysis of cache issues on the user experience</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-944">**Data.ChartType -** Zastarelo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-944">**Data.ChartType -** Obsolete</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationnewdocument"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-1213">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.NewDocument</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1213">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.NewDocument</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1214">Prikuplja se kada PowerPoint kreira novu prezentaciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1214">Collected when PowerPoint creates a new presentation.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="2505b-1215"> Uključuje metriku za uspeh, neuspeh i performanse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1215"> Includes success failure and performance metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1216">Ove informacije su potrebne da bismo proverili da li PowerPoint može uspešno da kreira datoteke bez degradacije u performansama.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1216">This information is used to ensure we can create files successfully and with no degradation in performance.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1217">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1217">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1218">**TipNovogDokumenta** – Da li je novi dokument kreiran iz predloška ili kreiran prazan?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1218">**NewDocumentType** – Whether new document is created from template or just created blank?</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1219">**FLifeguarded** – Da li dokument ima mogućnost samokorigovanja (funkcija koja sama ispravlja greške u dokumentu bez upita za korisnika)?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1219">**FLifeguarded** – Is document life guarded (feature that restores corrupt document state without prompting user)</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationopencompleteprotocol"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-1220">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.OpenCompleteProtocol</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1220">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.OpenCompleteProtocol</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1221">Prikuplja se kada PowerPoint otvori prezentacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1221">Collected when PowerPoint opens presentations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1222">Sadrži informacije koje su potrebne da bismo mogli pravilno da istražimo i dijagnostikujemo probleme koji se događaju na kraju procesa otvaranja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1222">It contains the information needed to be able to properly investigate and diagnose issues that happen through the end stages of the open process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1223">Microsoft koristi te podatke da bi se uverili da funkcija radi kao što je očekivano i ne postoji bilo kakva degradacija pri otvaranju prezentacija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1223">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and there is no degradation to opening presentations.</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsave"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-1279">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Save</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1279">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Save</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1280">Prikuplja se kad god PowerPoint vrši čuvanje pomoću moderne putanje kôda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1280">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a save using the modern code path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1281">Uključuje rezultat tipa uspeh ili neuspeh za metriku performansi pri čuvanju i odgovarajuće metapodatke dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1281">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1282"> Greške pri čuvanju mogu dovesti do gubitka podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1282"> Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1283">Microsoft koristi ove podatke da obezbedi da funkcija radi kao što je očekivano i da se uspešno vrši očuvanje korisničkog sadržaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1283">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsaveas"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-1364">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveAs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1364">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveAs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1365">Prikuplja se kad god PowerPoint izvršava komandu „Sačuvaj kao“</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1365">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a Save As.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1366">Uključuje rezultat tipa uspeh ili neuspeh za metriku performansi pri čuvanju i odgovarajuće metapodatke dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1366">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1367">Greške pri čuvanju mogu dovesti do gubitka podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1367">Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1368">Microsoft koristi ove podatke da obezbedi da funkcija radi kao što je očekivano i da se uspešno vrši očuvanje korisničkog sadržaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1368">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1369">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1369">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsavelegacy"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-1459">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveLegacy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1459">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveLegacy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1460">Prikuplja se kad god PowerPoint vrši čuvanje pomoću zastarele putanje kôda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1460">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a save using the legacy code path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1461">Uključuje rezultat tipa uspeh ili neuspeh za metriku performansi pri čuvanju i odgovarajuće metapodatke dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1461">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1462">Greške pri čuvanju mogu dovesti do gubitka podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1462">Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1463">Microsoft koristi ove podatke da obezbedi da funkcija radi kao što je očekivano i da se uspešno vrši očuvanje korisničkog sadržaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1463">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfilesaveactfconfirmsavedoccoreautorecoverysave"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-1887">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreAutoRecoverySave</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1887">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreAutoRecoverySave</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1888">Ovaj događaj ukazuje na to da Office Word čuva dokument sa automatskim oporavkom koji ranije nije sačuvan.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1888">This event indicates Office Word saves an auto-recovery document that has not been saved before.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1889">To omogućava korporaciji Microsoft da otkrije greške u automatskom oporavku, što je bitno za bezbednost dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1889">It allows Microsoft to detect errors in auto-recovery which is important for document data safety.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1890">Događaj prati da li automatski oporavak radi kao što je očekivano.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1890">The event monitors whether auto-recovery-save is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-1891">Takođe se koristi i za izračunavanje mesečno aktivnih korisnika/uređaja i metrike pouzdanosti oblaka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1891">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-1999">Ovaj događaj ukazuje na to da program Office Word čuva dokument kao nov.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-1999">This event indicates Office Word saves a document into a new document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2000">To omogućava korporaciji Microsoft da otkrije greške u funkciji „Sačuvaj kao“, što je bitno da bi se izbeglo gubljenje podataka u dokumentu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2000">It allows Microsoft to detect errors in save-as which is important to avoid document data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2001">Događaj prati da li funkcija „Sačuvaj kao“ radi kao što se očekuje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2001">The event monitors whether save-as is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2002">Takođe se koristi i za izračunavanje mesečno aktivnih korisnika/uređaja i metrike pouzdanosti oblaka. </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2002">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenifrinitargs"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-2747">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenIfrInitArgs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2747">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenIfrInitArgs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-2748">Ovaj događaj ukazuje na to da Office Word otvara dokument putem COM aktivacije ili komandne linije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2748">This event indicates Office Word opens a document via COM activation or command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2749">Sadrži i bitne podatke o performansama otvaranja datoteke i o tome da li je u pitanju događaj pokretanja aplikacije iz perspektive korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2749">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2750">Događaj prati da li otvaranje datoteke iz komandne linije radi kao što je očekivano.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2750">The event monitors whether file-open-from-command-line is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2751">Takođe se koristi i za izračunavanje mesečno aktivnih korisnika/uređaja i metrike pouzdanosti oblaka. </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2751">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-2752">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2752">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2753">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Izveštava da li smo u događaju mogli ispravno da unesemo druge vrednosti koje se tiču telemetrije dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2753">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Reports whether we were able to properly populate other document telemetry related values in the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2754">Koristi se za dijagnostiku kvaliteta podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2754">Used for data quality diagnostics.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2755">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Broj bajtova (komprimovanih) bez kojeg možemo da otvorimo datoteku ako ih preuzmemo pre nego što korisnik započne uređivanje ili čuvanje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2755">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we believe we can open the file without if we get them before the user wants to start editing or maybe saving.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenloadfile"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-2812">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenLoadFile</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2812">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenLoadFile</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-2813">Ovaj događaj ukazuje na to da Office Word otvara dokument putem dijaloga „Otvaranje“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2813">This event indicates Office Word opens a document via Open dialog.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2814">Sadrži i bitne podatke o performansama otvaranja datoteke i o tome da li je u pitanju događaj pokretanja aplikacije iz perspektive korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2814">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2815">Događaj prati da li otvaranje datoteke pomoću dijaloga „Otvaranje“ radi kao što je očekivano.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2815">The event monitors whether file-open-from-the-open-file-dialog is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2816">Takođe se koristi i za izračunavanje mesečno aktivnih korisnika/uređaja i metrike pouzdanosti oblaka. </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2816">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-2817">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2817">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2818">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Izveštava da li smo u događaju mogli ispravno da unesemo druge vrednosti koje se tiču telemetrije dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2818">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Reports whether we were able to properly populate other document telemetry related values in the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2819">Koristi se za dijagnostiku kvaliteta podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2819">Used for data quality diagnostics.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2820">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Broj bajtova (komprimovanih) bez kojeg možemo da otvorimo datoteku ako ih preuzmemo pre nego što korisnik započne uređivanje ili čuvanje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2820">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we believe we can open the file without if we get them before the user wants to start editing or maybe saving</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2821">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork -** Broj bajtova (komprimovanih) bez kojeg možda možemo da otvorimo dokument, ali potrebno je značajno investiranje u kôd da bi se to omogućilo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2821">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we might be able to open the file without but would require significant code investments to make it happen</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2822">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Broj bajtova (komprimovanih) koji moramo da imamo da bismo započeli otvaranje datoteke</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2822">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we must have before we can start opening the file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2823">**Data\_BytesUnknown -** Broj bajtova u segmentima dokumenta koji ne očekujemo da nađemo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2823">**Data\_BytesUnknown -** Number of bytes in document parts that we don’t expect to find</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2824">**Data\_DetachedDuration -** Koliko dugo je radnja odvojena od niti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2824">**Data\_DetachedDuration -** How long was the activity detached from the thread</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2825">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode -** Dokument je samo za čitanje/ili može da se uređuje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2825">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode -** Document is read only/editable</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="2505b-2826">**Data\_Doc\_AssistedReadingReasons -** Unapred definisani skup vrednosti koji se odnosi na razloge zbog kojih je dokument otvoren u režimu za čitanje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2826">**Data\_Doc\_AssistedReadingReasons -** Predefined set of values of why document was opened in assisted reading mode</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordaccessibilitylearningtoolsreadaloudplayreadaloud"></a><span data-ttu-id="2505b-2892">Office.Word.Accessibility.LearningTools.ReadAloud.PlayReadAloud</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-2892">Office.Word.Accessibility.LearningTools.ReadAloud.PlayReadAloud</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-3403">Prikuplja se svaki put kada program PowerPoint otkrije da nema internet veze.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-3403">Collected whenever PowerPoint detects there is no internet connectivity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2505b-3404">Microsoft koristi ove podatke da bi dobio dijagnostičke informacije o internet vezi korisnika u cilju razumevanja njenog uticaja na povezivanje sa uslugama sistema Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-3404">Microsoft uses this data to get diagnostic information about the user's internet connection to be able to understand how that impacts connectivity to Office services.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2505b-3405">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-3405">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2505b-3406">**Data\_IsNexusDetected:bool** - prikazuje da li imamo vezu sa internetom prilikom pozivanja usluge Nexus (vrednost tačno) ili prilikom pozivanja generičke veb usluge API (vrednost netačno)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2505b-3406">**Data\_IsNexusDetected:bool** - shows whether we got the Internet connectivity status when calling Nexus service (value true) or when calling generic web service API call (value false)</span></span>
